The prices of hundreds of yuan in normal times increased directly to two thousand yuan. This hotel is one of the few that did not increase the prices randomly. It is only about one hundred yuan more expensive than usual, and the price is very reasonable. The hotel is in the mountains, the air is good, and every service staff in it has a very good attitude. The child accidentally fell and injured, and two waiters came to comfort him, and also brought iodine and band-aids, and specially brought toys to comfort the child. It was really very thoughtful. There is also a special toiletries bag for children, which contains a little yellow duck soap, which the children like very much. After moving in, fruits and snacks were given, the room was very clean, and the front desk also specially upgraded the room with a terrace. I have stayed in many hotels in Dujiangyan and Qingcheng Mountain. This one has the highest comprehensive score in my mind. In addition, the geographical location is also very superior. It is within walking distance of Nanqiao and Lidui Park. There are many places to eat around, and my favorite Zhang Laozao headquarters is also very convenient. Oh, there is also a heated swimming pool and hot springs. It may be a bit cold in winter, but it is pretty good in other seasons. Everyone must come to this place when you come to Dujiangyan, I guarantee you won't be disappointed!
